<resp>None</resp><user_name>Ricardo Gomez< /user_name><Date>1503505330483< /Date><userid>110182917738621997554</userid><review>Another cozy, tiny hole-in-the-wall located just North of the railroad tracks, in a strip mall. I'm not sure when their busiest the most, but you probably want to call in your order instead, and take it home. Another option would be to take it with you to any of the local breweries and enjoy a nice cold beer with it, which is what I plan to do next time I visit. The dining area is maybe 6 feet by 10 feet at the most!! I think I counted 15 seats total. Lucky for my wife and I, we were able to sit down, enjoy our food, and watch a little preseason NFL in espa√±ol.

I ordered the Pan Con Chicharr√≥n and my wife ordered the Lomo Saltado plate. My "sandwich" was good, nothing out of the norm. It came with sweet potatoes and criolla. The meat was a little dry, but that's what you get with chicharron. Normally I wouldn't have ordered it, but apparently this is the popular sandwich on the menu. It's normally $6 but on Wednesdays it's $5. Some Peruvian places use bolillo bread for their sandwiches, but this place makes their sandwiches using ciabatta bread. It wasn't bad, but the bread makes a big difference. I asked my wife how her lomo saltado was and she responded with "I've had better." Don't get me wrong we still enjoyed the food very much (leftovers were bomb), but unfortunately for Micas, my wife and I have been spoiled to quite a bit of Peruvian places in the Inland Empire and Los Angeles.

Next time I visit Mica's I'm going to try their Jam√≥n Del Pa√≠s sandwich. It was the one I was originally going to try. I look forward to washing it down with a nice cold Inca Kola.< /review>< Rate>

<userid>None<//userid><name>Hotels.com reviewer<//name><Date>1618099200000<//Date><Rate>None<//Rate>< Review>
The Grove Inn is in a residential neighborhood and a good location. We had room 17, second floor, deluxe queen with bay windows. Not a spacious room but sufficient for our needs. I was having surgery at UCSF. Husband stayed 2 nights.  It was very clean, had been remodeled and deluxe bedding which was very comfortable for a good nights sleep.  Nice clean hot shower with new upgraded fixtures. About 10 pm a firetruck and some noisy cars came by and I thought it may be too noisy for me but after that, everything went quiet for the evening.  We felt very safe and saw no homeless on the streets close by. There was no alarm clock in the room therefore using my cell phone for that. Also because of covid, there was no breakfast service and they have a no contact checkin. We did not turn on the tv. There was a nice floor fan with several settings on it which we didn't need. The hosts were very accomodating and very pleasant to talk to on the phone. Even willing to switch our accomodations for a room with 2 beds had we needed it without add. charges. That was very kind of them. We would definitely stay here again. For us, location, safety, cleanliness, upgraded bedding, noise and parking fees were all factors in our decision to stay here. They did not disappoint.<//Review>

<user>105467977864636649645< /user><user_name>Christopher Bessette<//user_name><date>1569185044608</date><rate>5</rate><text>We were in San Francisco for a couple of days for an event at Civic Center Plaza and wanted to find a place within walking distance. I'm so glad we came across The Grove Inn! On our check-in day, we arrived early. The room wasn't available yet, but we were able to store our bags and one of the Inn attendants gave us restaurant and coffee shop recommendations.

We stayed in one of the upstairs rooms facing the street and it was very comfortable! The place has a unique "old house" feel to it, which was very cool. For breakfast, there was coffee, tea, orange juice, fresh bread from a local bakery, as well as other assorted breakfast items (cereal, oatmeal, etc.).

<review>This is a very sweet, but still clean and modern inn.  There is a continental breakfast that is more European than American, reminds me of a lot of breakfasts I had in hostels and hotels in Europe.  The breakfast isnt super impressive, but will be enough to fill you up for a day of sight seeing.  When we arrived, someone showed us our room but mentioned that there was a suite available if we would rather have that.  We were traveling with an infant, so we were thrilled to have the suite with an extra room so that we could still have a light/the tv on after the baby went to sleep.  The only negative was that the inn did not have any cribs, which was somewhat surprising.  However, luckily I had called ahead to ask about the crib so we were prepared, and rented a pack-n-play from a baby rental service.  But that is the only negative I would say about the inn, so if you dont need a crib, then I would highly recommend.  I loved the area it was in, and actually booked the inn after asking a friend who recently lived in San Francisco where to stay.  This was not a touristy area at all, but felt more like when you stay in an air bnb and are really in a neighborhood where locals hang out and live.<//review>< pictures>

< text>
Nice staff, great Tom Yum.

The actual restaurant has this interesting older character feel to it. I dont feel like I'm in La Habra when I'm inside. It feels more quaint urban. Like older New York.

I love this place! It's not much to look at, but the food is really good and the staff are super nice (if a bit weird - in a good way). Whenever we go in, one of the waiters always makes it a point to pick out a few magazines that he thinks we will like and brings them over to the table. Weird, but totally endearing. < Review>
This Michael's location in Serramonte shopping center is fun to shop. The store has it's standard picture frames and custom matting but what I found helpful is the clearance sections. The prices in the clearance section are discounted sometimes under 50%. The store also has a nice selection of crafts such as jewelery making, painting and silk screen.
The store seems to consistently have sales or online coupons.
The parking lot is shared between Target, BevMo, and Black Bear.<//Review>
